    <div class="cmp-accordion__item" data-cmp-hook-accordion="item" data-cmp-data-layer="{&quot;official-website-banner-item-3701712ce2&quot;:{&quot;@type&quot;:&quot;core/wcm/components/accordion/v1/accordion/item&quot;,&quot;dc:title&quot;:&quot;Official website.         <div class="cmp-accordion__header">
	  <h4>
            <button id="official-website-banner-item-3701712ce2-button" class="cmp-accordion__button" type="button" aria-controls="official-website-banner-item-3701712ce2-panel" data-cmp-hook-accordion="button" aria-expanded="false">
              <span class="cmp-accordion__icon"></span>
              <span class="cmp-accordion__title">Official website. How you know</span>
            </button>
	  </h4>
          
        </div>
        <div data-cmp-hook-accordion="panel" id="official-website-banner-item-3701712ce2-panel" class="cmp-accordion__panel cmp-accordion__panel--hidden" role="region" aria-labelledby="official-website-banner-item-3701712ce2-button" aria-hidden="true"><div class="container responsivegrid">

    
    <div id="container-844d085f09" class="cmp-container">
        


<div class="aem-Grid aem-Grid--12 aem-Grid--default--12 ">

        <div class="text">
<div data-cmp-data-layer="{&quot;text-a4cbfd3690&quot;:{&quot;@type&quot;:&quot;nycgov/components/text&quot;,&quot;repo:modifyDate&quot;:&quot;2024-09-18T18:55:29Z&quot;,&quot;xdm:text&quot;:&quot;&lt;h5&gt;&lt;b&gt;Official websites use .gov&lt;/b&gt;&lt;/h5&gt;\r\n&lt;p&gt;A .gov website belongs to an official government organization in the United States.&lt;/p&gt;\r\n&quot;}}" id="text-a4cbfd3690" class="cmp-text ">
    <h5><b>Official websites use .gov</b></h5>
<p>A .gov website belongs to an official government organization in the United States.</p>

</div>

    

</div>
<div class="text">
<div data-cmp-data-layer="{&quot;text-ec59d1af32&quot;:{&quot;@type&quot;:&quot;nycgov/components/text&quot;,&quot;repo:modifyDate&quot;:&quot;2024-09-27T19:32:19Z&quot;,&quot;xdm:text&quot;:&quot;&lt;h5&gt;&lt;b&gt;Secure .gov websites use HTTPS&lt;/b&gt;&lt;/h5&gt;\r\n&lt;p&gt;A lock (&amp;#x1f512;) or https:// means you’ve safely connected to the .gov website. Share sensitive information only on official, secure websites.&lt;/p&gt;\r\n&quot;}}" id="text-ec59d1af32" class="cmp-text ">
    <h5><b>Secure .gov websites use HTTPS</b></h5>
<p>A lock (🔒) or https:// means you’ve safely connected to the .gov website. Share sensitive information only on official, secure websites.</p>

</div>

    

</div>

  <script>
   const isSearchPage = document.body.classList.contains("searchpage");
   const isMainSite = document.body.classList.contains("main-site");
   const customSearchBox = document.querySelector('#coveo-search-btn-redirect custom-search-box');
   const mainHost = customSearchBox?.getAttribute("data-search-url");
   if (!isMainSite) {
     const searchBoxes = document.querySelectorAll('custom-search-box[data-search-url]');
     const url = new URL(window.location.href);
     const host = url.host;
     const pathSegments = url.pathname.split('/').filter(Boolean);
     const isoCodeRegex = /^[a-z]{2}(-[A-Z]{2})?$/;
     const isSameHost = mainHost.includes(host);
     const searchPageHost = new URL(mainHost).host;
     const isSameDomain = (host === searchPageHost);
     let site = host;
     if (isSameHost) {
       const relevantSegment = isoCodeRegex.test(pathSegments[0]) ? pathSegments[1] : pathSegments[0] || '';
       site = host + "/" + relevantSegment;
     }
     customSearchBox.setAttribute('is-external-domain', !isSameDomain);
     searchBoxes.forEach(box => {
       const currentUrl = box.getAttribute('data-search-url');
       const newUrl = currentUrl + "?sitesearch=" + site;
       box.setAttribute('data-search-url', newUrl);
     });
   }
   if (isSearchPage) {
     const redirectEl = document.getElementById("coveo-search-btn-redirect");
     if (redirectEl) { redirectEl.remove(); }
   } else {
     const resultsEl = document.getElementById("coveo-search-btn-results");
     if (resultsEl) { resultsEl.remove(); }
   }
  </script>

<div id="teaser-d887856f10" class="cmp-teaser" data-cmp-data-layer="{&quot;teaser-d887856f10&quot;:{&quot;@type&quot;:&quot;core/wcm/components/teaser/v2/teaser&quot;,&quot;repo:modifyDate&quot;:&quot;2026-03-13T17:48:07Z&quot;,&quot;dc:title&quot;:&quot;Learn about vaccination&quot;,&quot;dc:description&quot;:&quot;&lt;p&gt;&lt;span class=\&quot;small-paragraph\&quot;&gt;What’s happening?&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;\r\n&lt;p&gt;Getting your child vaccinated as early as possible can save their life.     <p class="cmp-teaser__pretitle">March 13, 2026</p>

            
    <h3 class="cmp-teaser__title">
        Learn about vaccination
    </h3>

            
    <div class="cmp-teaser__description"><p><span class="small-paragraph">What’s happening?</span></p>
<p>Getting your child vaccinated as early as possible can save their life. Find answers to questions about childhood vaccines and what you can do to protect your child.</p>
<p><span class="small-paragraph">Who’s it for?</span></p>
<p>Parents of babies, kids, and teens</p>

    <h3 class="cmp-teaser__title">
        Heat season
    </h3>

            
    <div class="cmp-teaser__description"><p><span class="small-paragraph">What's happening?</span></p>
<p>It's cold! Building owners are legally required to provide heat from October 1st to May 31st when temperatures are chilly.</p>
<p><span class="small-paragraph">Who's it for?</span></p>
<p>All New Yorkers</p>
